&lt;div align="left"&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Summary&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test completes the Book Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
The test is the reusable template (other tests can contain a call to it in order to guide a user through 
the Book Flight page 
completion procedure).&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Description&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test is composed of the following stages:&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;ol style="margin-top: 0mm; margin-bottom: 0mm; "&gt;

Flight page form completion.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt; 
Secure Purchase execution.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

&lt;div align="left"&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Summary&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test completes the Flight Finder page forms, selects the flight on the Select Flight page, and completes 
the certain sections 
of the Book Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
The test is the reusable template (other tests can contain a call to it in order to guide a user through 
the procedures preceding 
the flight booking).&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Description&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test is composed of the following stages:&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;ol style="margin-top: 0mm; margin-bottom: 0mm; "&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;Specification 
of Flight Details and Preferences on the Find Flight page.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;Flight 
selection from the available flights list on the Select Flight page.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;Completion 
of the certain sections on the Book Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Test Calls&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Find Flight: &amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; &amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;Specification 
of Flight Details and Preferences on the Find Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Select Flight: &amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; &amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;Flight selection from the available flights 
list in the Select Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Parameters&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font

&lt;div align="left"&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Summary&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test verifies the Billing and Delivery Address sections on the Book Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Description&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test is composed of the following stages:&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;ol style="margin-top: 0mm; margin-bottom: 0mm; "&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;&amp;nbsp;Connection 
to Mercury Tours application and sign on.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt; 
Execution of the preparation steps that lead the user to the Book Flight page.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt; 
Verification of Billing and Delivery Address sections completed with the different values.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Test Calls&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Connect and 
Sign On:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Connection to Mercury 
Tours application and sign on using your username and password.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Book Flight 
Preparation:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Specification 
of Flight Details and Preferences on the Find Flight page. &lt;br /&gt;
Flight selection from the available flights list on the Select Flight page. &lt;br /&gt;
Completion of the certain sections on the Book Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

&lt;div align="left"&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Summary&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test verifies the user interface of the Book Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Description&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test is composed of the following stages:&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;ol style="margin-top: 0mm; margin-bottom: 0mm; "&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;Connection 
to Mercury Tours application and sign on.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;Execution 
of the preparation steps that lead the user to the Book Flight page.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="font-family: Arial;  color: #010101;  "&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt; font-family:Arial; color:#010101; font-weight:Normal; font-style:Normal; font-decoration:Normal"&gt;Execution 
of the standard web page verifications (Spelling, order, fonts, menus, grammar, etc.).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;div align="left"&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#008000"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;To understand standard 
web page verifications, please refer to the called test description.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span 
style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Test Calls&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Connect and 
Sign On:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Connection to Mercury Tours 
application and sign on using your username and password.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Find Flight:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Specification of Flight Details and Preferences on the Find 
Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Select Flight:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Flight selection from the available flights list on the Select 
Flight page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;HTML Page 
Layout:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; HTML page layout verification.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Menus:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Page menus verification.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Forms:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Page form and form elements (lists, radio buttons and input 
fields) verification.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Spelling 
&amp;amp; Grammar:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Page spelling 
and grammar verification.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Tab Order:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; Tab order verification on the page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#000080" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;HTML page 
source:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt; HTML page source verification.&lt;br /&gt;

&lt;div align="left"&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Summary&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test verifies the Departing and Arriving Location selection on the Flight Finder page.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font face="Arial" color="#800000" size="+0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:10pt"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Description&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;font 
face="Arial"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size:8pt"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The test is composed of the following stages:&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
